Set activations and weights flags.\n24:         qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n25: \n26:         # Make sure _all returns True when asked for both ACTIVATIONS and INT8_WEIGHTS.\n27:         self.assertTrue(qm._all(QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS))\n28:         # Test weight only (int4).\n61:         qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, False, False, False, False, True)\n62:         # Make sure only the INT4_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n63:         self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS)\n64: \n65:         # Test weight only.\n66:         qm = QuantMode.use_weight_only(use_int4_weights=True)\n67:         # Make sure only the INT4_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n68:         self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS)\n69: \n70:         # Test activation/weight per-tensor.\n71:         qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, True, False, False)\n72:         # The reference.\n73:         expected_qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n74:         # Make sure all flags are set.\n104:         self.assertEqual(qm, expected_qm)\n105: \n106:     def test_per_channel(self):\n107:         # Set per-channel flag.\n108:         qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS | QuantMode.PER_CHANNEL\n109:         # Make sure it returns True for per-channel.\n110:         self.assertTrue(qm.has_per_channel_scaling())\n111:         # Do not set per-channel flag.\n112:         qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n113:         # Make sure it returns False for per-channel.\n114:         self.assertFalse(qm.has_per_channel_scaling())\n115: \n116:     def test_per_token(self):\n117:         # Set per-token flag.\n118:         qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS | QuantMode.PER_TOKEN\n119:         # Do not set per-token flag.\n125:         qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n126:         # Make sure it returns False for per-token.\n127:         self.assertFalse(qm.has_per_token_dynamic_scaling())\n128:         # Make sure it returns True for per-tensor.\n129:         self.assertTrue(qm.has_act_static_scaling())\n130: \n131:     def test_weights_only(self):\n132:         # Set weights flags.\n133:         qm = QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n134:         # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n135:         self.assertTrue(qm.is_weight_only())\n136:         # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n137:         self.assertTrue(qm.is_int8_weight_only())\n138: \n139:         # has_act_static_scaling(self):\n        return not self.has_per_token_dynamic_scaling(\n        ) and not self.has_fp8_rowwise()\n\n    def has_per_channel_scaling(self):\n        return self._any(self.PER_CHANNEL)\n\n    def has_per_group_scaling(self):\n        return self._any(self.PER_GROUP)\n\n    def has_int8_kv_cache(self):\n        return self._any(self.INT8_KV_CACHE)\n\n
